    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold; text-align: center;">SANUWAVE Announces Q1 FY2024 Financial Results</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-align: center;">&#160; <br>
    </div>
    <div>
      <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic; text-align: center;">Q1 2024 revenues were $5.8 million, up 53% from Q1 2023</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-align: center;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic; text-align: center;">Q1 2024 gross margin was 73%, up 600bp from Q1 2023</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-align: center;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic; text-align: center;">Operating loss was $1.1 million for Q1 2024 compared to $2.0 million for Q1 2023</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-align: center;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic; text-align: center;">Company provides guidance for revenue growth of 45-55% for Q2 2024 versus Q2 2023 and reiterates revenue growth guidance of 50% for FY 2024 compared
        to FY 2023</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    </div>
    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(29, 34, 40);">EDEN PRAIRIE, MN, May 10, 2024 (GLOBE </font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">NEWSWIRE) -- via </font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">NewMediaWire</font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> -- </font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Sanuwave Health, Inc.</font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> (the "Company" or "Sanuwave&#8221;) (OTCQB:
        SNWV), a leading provider of next-generation </font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(29, 34, 40);">FDA-approved wound care products, </font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">is pleased to provide its financial
        results for the three months ended March 31, 2024.</font></div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Q1 2024 ended March 31, 2024</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="zd4af2b32eb364c008b1022e553dff3c1" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">Revenue for the three months ended March 31, 2024, totaled $5.8 million, an increase of 53%, as compared to $3.8 million for the same period of 2023.&#160; This growth is within the previous guidance for
              a 45 &#8211; 55% increase.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z37ec25dd2bdb448ca0db1d60173fe453" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">43 UltraMist&#174; systems were sold in Q1 2024, up from 28 in Q1 2023, and down from 79 in Q4 2023.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z9f358917192a4d038ff47a06e32ffc71" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">UltraMist&#174; consumables revenue increased by 64% to $4.1 million (71% of revenues) in Q1 2024, versus $2.5 million for the same quarter last year. UltraMIST systems and consumables remained the
              primary revenue growth driver and continued to represent in excess of 90% of SANUWAVE&#8217;s overall revenues in Q1 2024.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z54ea88b6bfa44ce6bab8c3f4c6920dca" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">Gross margin as a percentage of revenue amounted to 73% for the three months ended March 31, 2024, vs. 67% for the same period last year, driven by the increase in average selling price of UltraMist&#174;
              and stabilization of cost of sales in 2024.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z10d483184e3743a6be367cbea099766c" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>

            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">For the three months ended March 31, 2024, operating loss totaled $1.1 million, an improvement of $0.9 million compared to Q1 2023 as a result of the Company&#8217;s continued efforts to drive profitable
              growth and manage expenses.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="zf31eb094b8a84f838dd66b791d91e545" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">

          </td>
        </tr>

            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">Adjusted EBITDA <sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">1</sup> loss for the three months ended March 31, 2024, was $59 thousand versus an Adjusted EBITDA loss of $1.8 million for the same period last year, an improvement of $1.7
              million.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">1</sup>&#160;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">This is a non-GAAP financial measure.         information.</font></div>

    </div>
    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8220;The first quarter showed an acceleration in year over year revenue growth rate for Sanuwave as we start to see the results of all the hard work put in on manufacturing, operations, and
      increasingly sales,&#8221; said Morgan Frank, CEO.&#160; &#8220;This was the best first quarter in Company history by a wide margin, and Adjusted EBITDA remained near break-even level despite some meaningful non-recurring costs in the quarter.&#160; Like much of the life
      science and medical device space, the first quarter is a seasonally slower time for Sanuwave, but this did not stop us from accelerating our growth rate and setting the groundwork to build and sustain this higher growth.&#160; We hired four new
      salespeople in the quarter and are looking to hire more going forward.&#160; We aim for 2024 to be the breakout year for Sanuwave.&#8221;</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Financial Outlook</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The Company forecasts Q2 2024 revenue to rise 45-55% vs Q2 2023 and for gross margin as a percentage of revenue to remain in the mid 70s.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Our merger with SEPA remains ongoing and active.&#160; We&#8217;re continuing to work toward finalizing the exchange listing and the Company believes it sees a path to closing this transaction in May.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">SANUWAVE's end-to-end wound care portfolio of regenerative medicine products and product candidates helps restore the body&#8217;s normal healing processes. SANUWAVE applies and researches its
      patented energy transfer technologies in wound healing, orthopedic/spine, aesthetic/cosmetic, and cardiac/endovascular conditions.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div>
      <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Non-GAAP Financial Measures</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">This press release includes certain financial measures that are not presented in our financial statements prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United
        States (U.S.) (&#8220;U.S. GAAP&#8221;). These financial measures are considered "non-GAAP financial measures" and are intended to supplement, and should not be considered as superior to, or a replacement for, financial measures presented in accordance with
        U.S. GAAP.</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The Company uses Earnings Before Interest, Taxes, Depreciation and Amortization (&#8220;EBITDA&#8221;) and Adjusted EBITDA to assess its operating performance. Adjusted EBITDA is Earnings before
        Interest, Taxes, Depreciation and Amortization adjusted for the change in fair value of derivatives and any significant non-cash or infrequent charges.&#160; EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA should not be considered as alternatives to net loss as a measure of
        financial performance or any other performance measure derived in accordance with GAAP, and they should not be construed as an inference that the Company&#8217;s future results will be unaffected by unusual or infrequent items. These non-GAAP financial
        measures are presented in a consistent manner for each period, unless otherwise disclosed. The Company uses these measures for the purpose of evaluating its historical and prospective financial performance, as well as its performance relative to
        competitors. These measures also help the Company to make operational and strategic decisions. The Company believes that providing this information to investors, in addition to GAAP measures, allows them to see the Company&#8217;s results through the
        eyes of management, and to better understand its historical and future financial performance. These non-GAAP financial measures are also frequently used by analysts, investors, and other interested parties to evaluate companies in our industry,
        when considered alongside other GAAP measures.</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA have their limitations as analytical tools, and you should not consider them in isolation or as a substitute for analysis of the Company&#8217;s results as reported
        under GAAP. Some of these limitations are that EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA:</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    </div>
    <div>

          <tr>
            <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
            </td>
